    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer11154735167315289339">The book provides some powerful Om chanting and meditation techniques to bring balance health and harmony in life. In Eastern religions, Om (AUM) is considered as the most sacred mantra. Om is the mantra of integration; integration of individual with the Whole. Om is the mantra of harmony and celebration. Om is the mantra to access the Supreme Divinity residing within us. </span>
  <span id="freeText11154735167315289339" style="display:none">The book provides some powerful Om chanting and meditation techniques to bring balance health and harmony in life. In Eastern religions, Om (AUM) is considered as the most sacred mantra. Om is the mantra of integration; integration of individual with the Whole. Om is the mantra of harmony and celebration. Om is the mantra to access the Supreme Divinity residing within us. In this book Amit Ray describes several Om chanting and Om meditation methods in detail in a lucid and plain English. Om chanting and meditations have healing effects on the body and the mind. This book is a step-by-step guide to practise meditations with the Om. As you practise, a long-lasting sense of well-being manifests in your life. You will notice a sense of joyfulness entering your life along with an ability to appreciate the many gifts that surround you. This book will help both the beginners as well as the advanced practitioners.</span>

<div id="review_468688803" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/468688803" />
    <a title="Angela Powell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15121121-angela-powell"><img alt="Angela Powell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1354511799p2/15121121.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/468688803?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela Powell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela Powell" href="/user/show/15121121-angela-powell">Angela Powell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9788191026931" href="/book/show/8596505-om-chanting-meditation">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15121121-angela-powell?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15121121-angela-powell?shelf=meditation">meditation</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer468688803" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14331325855160498213">I am so pleased to have found this book. The spirit of the book is extraordinary. I feel, this book is a great gift of God to me. I believe that Dr. Ray has the unique talent for offering teaching which is simple yet profound, supremely practical and yet deeply spiritual. <br/><br/>The eternal flame of Self is located in our spiritual heart. Om meditation and remembering is the path to reach that eternal flame. The experience of the divine self is so powerful that the experiencer feel one with the absolut</span>
  <span id="freeText14331325855160498213" style="display:none">I am so pleased to have found this book. The spirit of the book is extraordinary. I feel, this book is a great gift of God to me. I believe that Dr. Ray has the unique talent for offering teaching which is simple yet profound, supremely practical and yet deeply spiritual. <br /><br />The eternal flame of Self is located in our spiritual heart. Om meditation and remembering is the path to reach that eternal flame. The experience of the divine self is so powerful that the experiencer feel one with the absolute. When the experience is authentic all the spiritual questions are answered and great truths are revealed. <br /><br />The subtle energy of the book overwhelmed me. This book is a great expression of God's love to me.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14465055867231408901">Almost from my childhood I am accustomed to Om. Earlier, it hardly penetrated my consciousness. I listened to it on every occasion, but unnoticed. Normally, at the beginning of any mantra Om is added. I was thinking I know everything about Om. But after reading this book slowly my understanding changed.   <span id="freeText14465055867231408901" style="display:none">Almost from my childhood I am accustomed to Om. Earlier, it hardly penetrated my consciousness. I listened to it on every occasion, but unnoticed. Normally, at the beginning of any mantra Om is added. I was thinking I know everything about Om. But after reading this book slowly my understanding changed. Last few months I am doing Om meditation and now I realize it’s depth. Om increased the levels of my awareness and with higher level of awareness I get more clarity of mind and now, I can make wiser choices in life. I love Om meditation because it is easy and it is free from any Guru or Organization. There is no complicated process, I just need to sit down and peacefully chant few Oms according to my pace. There is no hurry in it. I have a choice to do other Om meditations according to my liking. Earlier, I was too serious and stressed on everything. Now I can focus more on every aspect of life with peace and tranquility. Now life is a pure joy of helping self and helping others. Now I understand other dimensions of life. Now I know every set back is a seed for another grand opportunity. Sometimes I focus on the Godliness aspect of Om and I cultivate love. I expand my heart. Om has given me the power to accommodate and accept others. Moreover, I feel the protection and healing power of Om. Now, I am free from fears and confusions and my consciousness is free from clouds. The most wonderful part of this book is its simplicity. Many thanks to Dr. Ray for this wonderful gift of love.</span>

From the first few pages I knew that he would become one of my favorite authors because he doesn't try to fill my head with nonsense, but instead encourages us by introducing new ways of thinking and being more open minded. I am very happy to discovered this book. </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('yDKB4V+fUvs9gtj5GoBmadkIx2NqXZ4KTfz8LQaJKpHyFOgz5MGbk5qpbJjtdWy2D1cgq6TQEG0Wgrqcy8rYCw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OLu+q70dooElwXjCj5fIcT9slMffH2uQHTlOcjQt460Cndd5BkNr6YLqzKN4YsKu6TNzDxGS5fdGRwjD+W4RNw==')})
  }

His observations and insights are plain, practical, and down-to-earth, and they deal exclusively with the present. <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer948951536744983935">Amit Ray is an enlightened spiritual master in the Himalayan Yoga and Vipassana tradition. He is also famous for his contribution on Quantum Computing and Artificial Intelligence. He began sharing his experiences after a series of transformative spiritual awakening. He is a man who attained complete realization of the Infinite. He is a man of compassion and love.<br/>In his Himalayan Centre at Uttarkas</span>
  <span id="freeText948951536744983935" style="display:none">Amit Ray is an enlightened spiritual master in the Himalayan Yoga and Vipassana tradition. He is also famous for his contribution on Quantum Computing and Artificial Intelligence. He began sharing his experiences after a series of transformative spiritual awakening. He is a man who attained complete realization of the Infinite. He is a man of compassion and love.<br />In his Himalayan Centre at Uttarkashi, he lives a life dedicated to meditation and yoga. He is author of several books on meditation, compassion, yoga, quantum computing, Artificial Intelligence and other topics. <br />Amit Ray, as a scientist, after doing his PhD in artificial intelligence and computational neuroscience, conducted many research in the areas of intelligence, quantum theory and the nature of consciousness. He worked in India, USA and UK for about 15 years. He has implemented many complex and large-scale AI projects across the world. With a spiritual bent of mind from his very childhood, he undertook intense practices in meditation from when he was a child. In his later years, many mystical experiences prompted him to dedicate his life for the search of truth. He taught that true freedom is possible for everyone of us. </span>
